### [113] [LLMSurgeon: Diagnosing Data Mixture of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30348)
*Yaxin Luo,Jiacheng Cui,Xiaohan Zhao,Xinyi Shang,Jiacheng Liu,Xinyue Bi,Zhaoyi Li,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了LLMSurgeon框架，旨在通过模型生成的文本反推大语言模型的预训练数据构成，为黑盒模型提供了一种无需原始训练数据的有效审计方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的预训练数据构成其核心能力，但目前模型通常不公开训练数据构成，导致难以对模型进行事后审计。研究旨在解决如何仅通过分析目标模型生成的文本，反向推断其预训练语料的领域分布（即数据混合手术，DMS）这一难题。

Method: 提出了一种名为“LLMSurgeon”的框架，将数据混合重构问题转化为基于标签偏移假设（label-shift assumption）的逆问题。该方法不直接聚合分类器输出，而是构建了一个校准的软混淆矩阵（soft confusion matrix），并求解约束逆问题，从而修正领域混淆并恢复潜在的数据分布。同时，开发了名为“LLMScan”的验证套件进行评估。

Result: 在LLMScan验证套件（使用具有透明训练数据的开源LLM构建）上的实验表明，LLMSurgeon能够以高保真度恢复预训练数据的领域混合比例，证明了其在模型审计任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在无需访问原始训练数据的情况下，通过分析模型生成的文本，可以高精度地反推其预训练数据的领域分布。这为提升大语言模型的透明度和审计能力提供了实用的技术路径。

Abstract: The pretraining data mixture of Large Language Models (LLMs) constitutes their "digital DNA", shaping model behaviors, capabilities, and failure modes. Yet this composition is rarely disclosed, making post-hoc auditing of data combination or provenance difficult. In this work, we formalize $\textbf{Data Mixture Surgery (DMS)}$: given only generated text from a target LLM, estimate the domain-level distribution of its pretraining corpus under a predefined taxonomy. We propose $\textbf{LLMSurgeon}$, a strong framework that casts DMS as an inverse problem under the label-shift assumption. Rather than directly aggregating classifier outputs, LLMSurgeon estimates a calibrated $\textit{soft}$ confusion matrix and solves a constrained inverse problem to correct systematic domain confusion and recover the latent mixture prior. To evaluate, we introduce $\textbf{LLMScan}$, a recipe-verifiable evaluation suite built from open-source LLMs with transparent pretraining mixtures. Across LLMScan, LLMSurgeon recovers domain mixtures with high fidelity under fixed protocols. Our work presents a practical, post-hoc approach for auditing the digital DNA of foundation models without access to their training data.

</details>


### [114] [Unlocking the Working Memory of Large Language Models for Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30343)
*Lukas Aichberger,Sepp Hochreiter*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了提高大模型的推理效率，该论文提出了“推理在记忆中”（RiM）方法，利用固定的特殊记忆块替代自动生成的推理链，实现了在单次前向传递中完成潜在推理，从而在保持高性能的同时显著提升了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的提升大模型推理能力的方法通常依赖于生成中间推理令牌（Chain-of-Thought），这导致推理过程与外部输出耦合，增加了计算开销并混淆了内部计算与外部通信。受人类认知中利用工作记忆进行内部处理的启发，研究者旨在开发一种无需自回归生成中间步骤、更加高效的“潜在推理”（latent reasoning）方法。

Method: 引入了一种名为“推理在记忆中”（Reasoning in Memory, RiM）的方法，该方法使用一组固定的特殊令牌序列作为“记忆块”来替代自回归生成的中间推理步骤。具体实现分为两个阶段：第一阶段通过在记忆块后预测显式的推理步骤来进行“接地”（grounding）训练；第二阶段则移除显式推理监督，直接通过在记忆块后迭代优化最终答案。这种方法允许模型在单次前向传递中处理推理任务。

Result: 在多个推理基准测试中，RiM在不同规模和架构的大模型上均表现出优异性能，能够匹配甚至超过现有的潜在推理方法，同时显著降低了计算复杂性，避免了长序列推理带来的生成开销。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型可以通过训练使用“工作记忆”机制进行有效的潜在推理。RiM方法证明了无需生成显式的中间推理步骤，即可通过固定长度的特殊记忆块实现高效的推理计算，这为提升模型的推理能力提供了一种更具计算效率的新范式。

Abstract: To improve the reasoning capabilities of large language models, test-time compute is typically scaled by generating intermediate tokens before the final answer. However, this couples reasoning to autoregressive generation and thereby conflates internal computation with external communication. In contrast, human cognition can use working memory to hold and manipulate information internally without the need to externalize intermediate thoughts. Drawing on this principle, we introduce Reasoning in Memory (RiM), a latent reasoning method that replaces the autoregressive generation of reasoning steps with memory blocks. These memory blocks are fixed sequences of special tokens that unlock the working-memory capacity of large language models. Since they are fixed rather than generated, they can be processed in a single forward pass, enabling compute-efficient latent reasoning. To operationalize these memory blocks, we employ a two-stage curriculum. First, we ground them by predicting explicit reasoning steps after each memory block. Second, we discard this step-level supervision and iteratively refine the final answer after each memory block. Our experiments on reasoning benchmarks show that, across language models of different families and sizes, RiM matches or exceeds existing latent reasoning methods while avoiding the autoregressive generation of thoughts. These results demonstrate that large language models can be trained to use working memory as an effective mechanism for latent reasoning.

</details>

### [115] [Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation via Implicit Reasoning in Amap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28888)
*Sicong Wang,Ruiting Dong,Yue Liu,Bowen Zheng,Jun Meng,Jie Li,Shuaijun Guo,Yu Gu,Fanyi Di,Xin Li*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对生成式时空意图推荐任务，GPlan 通过将大模型的推理逻辑蒸馏至轻量模型并引入反事实对齐机制，解决了工业部署中高延迟与物理约束不可行的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界中的用户行为具有时空依赖性，现有大语言模型在生成意图序列推荐（GSISR）任务中存在推理延迟高、计划缺乏物理可行性及上下文不匹配等问题，难以满足工业级部署需求。

Method: 1. 渐进式隐式思维链蒸馏（Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation）：将大模型的推理逻辑压缩到隐空间令牌（latent tokens）中，使小模型在无需输出冗长文本的情况下继承推理能力。
2. 时空反事实直接偏好优化（Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO）：通过构造反事实样本对模型进行对齐，增强模型对时空上下文的敏感度，减少违背物理约束的计划。

Result: 离线评估和线上A/B测试结果表明，GPlan 显著提升了推荐意图序列的连贯性与上下文响应能力，同时满足了低延迟的工业应用标准。

Conclusion: GPlan 通过知识蒸馏和对比学习技术，成功将大语言模型的复杂推理能力迁移至轻量级模型中，在保证实时响应的同时，显著提升了生成意图序列的逻辑连贯性和时空约束匹配度。

Abstract: Real-world user behavior rarely consists of isolated actions; instead, it often forms intent flows governed by spatiotemporal dependencies. To provide integrated service recommendations, we focus on the task of Generative Spatiotemporal Intent Sequence Recommendation (GSISR), which aims to generate intent sequences that are logically coherent and physically executable within complex spatiotemporal contexts. While LLMs offer strong reasoning potential for GSISR, direct industrial deployment is limited by high inference latency and context-mismatched or physically infeasible plans. To address these challenges, we propose a generative framework, GPlan, that internalizes LLM reasoning into lightweight models through two components. First, to enable reasoning under strict latency constraints, we introduce Progressive Implicit CoT Distillation, which compresses explicit reasoning processes into reserved latent tokens, allowing small models to inherit complex planning logic without generating long reasoning text. Second, to address the disconnect between general knowledge and real-world constraints, we design Spatiotemporal Counterfactual DPO. By aligning the model with counterfactual context-plan pairs, we improve sensitivity to spatiotemporal context and reduce context-mismatched plans. Offline experiments and online A/B testing demonstrate that our approach improves sequence coherence and context responsiveness. Our implementation and the anonymized GSISR dataset are available at https://github.com/alibaba/GPlan.

</details>


### [116] [Toward User Preference Alignment in LLM Recommendation via Explicit Context Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29141)
*Weizhi Zhang,Wooseong Yang,Yuxin Cui,Zhaohui Guo,Hins Hu,Liangwei Yang,Henry Peng Zou,Qifei Wang,Hanqing Zeng,Jiayi Liu,Yinglong Xia,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对现有推荐系统忽视用户显式反馈（评论文本）的问题，本文倡导将此类上下文信息作为LLM推荐系统的核心，以通过深入的语义理解来优化用户偏好对齐，改善推荐的个性化与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统推荐系统过度依赖隐式行为信号，忽略了用户通过文本表达的显式上下文反馈（如评论、评价），导致系统难以捕捉用户行为背后的语义逻辑，从而产生用户偏好对齐偏差，并加剧“过滤气泡”效应。现有LLM推荐系统也多局限于利用元数据，未能充分挖掘用户生成的丰富文本内容。

Method: 本文采用综述与框架设计相结合的方法：首先回顾了推荐系统范式的演进，分析了显式上下文反馈的价值；随后提出了整合此类异构用户信号至可扩展LLM驱动推荐系统的新型框架，并呼吁建立针对性的评估基准与指标。

Result: 文章确立了以“用户偏好建模”为核心的下一代推荐系统愿景，明确了显式上下文反馈在提升推荐质量、多样性和可解释性方面的重要潜力，并为构建更透明的在线推荐平台提供了理论框架和技术指引。

Conclusion: 本文强调了显式上下文反馈（如用户评论和反馈文本）在下一代LLM推荐系统中的核心地位，指出整合此类信息不仅能提升推荐的准确性和个性化程度，还能增强系统的透明度与可解释性，是打破算法信息茧房的关键方向。

Abstract: Traditional recommender systems (RecSys) primarily infer user preferences from implicit signals (such as clicks, watches, and purchases), often neglecting the rich explicit contextual feedback users provide through verbal text, like comments and reviews. This explicit context feedback captures the nuanced reasons behind user decisions regarding their preferences. In addition, it offers critical heterogeneous information for user preference alignment and more explainable recommendations. Overlooking such signals can lead to misaligned user preferences and further reinforce filter bubbles, as algorithms fail to understand the "semantic context" behind user choices. Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) present new opportunities to harness user-generated content for more accurate and diverse recommendations, yet current LLM-based recommendations still focus on using item meta-data and underutilize this resource. In this paper, we advocate for prioritizing explicit context feedback in the next generation of LLM-based RecSys. We review the evolution of recommendation paradigms, highlight the value of context-rich feedback, call for new benchmarks and metrics, and introduce frameworks for integrating explicit user signals into scalable LLM-driven RecSys. Centering on user-preference modeling, we aim to foster more personalized, transparent, and explainable RecSys online platforms.

### [117] [On the Practice of Scaling Search Conversion Rate Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29232)
*James Pak,Jyun-Yu Jiang,Fan Zhang,Sen Wang,Taekmin Kim,Henry Tsai,Vijay Rajaram,Juexin Lin,Mohitdeep Singh,Alessandro Magnani,Johnny Chen,Qian Zhao,Rao Fu,Zhirong Liang,Jordan Gilliland,Winter Jiao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一套高效缩放搜索CVR预测模型的方法，通过系统化地调整模型规模、数据量及采用先进的工程优化技术，成功在不增加推理延迟的前提下，实现了模型性能的显著提升和业务指标的增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在处理高流量搜索环境时，现有的转化率（CVR）预测模型面临严峻挑战：如何在提升模型预测精度（质量）的同时，严格控制训练成本并满足生产环境对推理延迟的严苛要求。

Method: 1. 经验性缩放研究：分析模型骨干计算量、嵌入参数规模和训练数据量对模型质量的影响；2. 架构评估：在真实大规模电商数据集上评估多种前沿架构及其集成；3. 训练优化：采用简化的“热启动”（warmstart）策略以加速迭代；4. 推理优化：应用解耦图执行（decoupled graph execution）和动态批处理（dynamic batching）技术以满足低延迟要求。

Result: 通过优化，最终部署的模型使用了2.5倍于基准的训练数据，推理计算量增加了8倍，且几乎未对延迟产生负面影响。线上A/B测试显示，该模型使核心搜索转化率指标提升了2.6%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在保证低延迟的前提下，通过系统性的缩放策略（模型骨干、参数规模及数据量）显著提升搜索转化率预测模型的性能是可行的。研究结论强调了各缩放因素的独立性，并提供了一套适用于大规模生产环境的工程优化方案。

Abstract: Scaling a Search Conversion Rate (CVR) prediction model, especially in high-traffic environments, presents a challenge: superior model quality needs to be balanced with strict constraints on training cost and serving latency. This paper details an effective approach for scaling modern search CVR prediction models. We begin with an empirical study to understand the scaling performance of search CVR models, analyzing how quality improves as we scale three key factors of model backbone computation, the size of embedding parameters, and the volume of training data.
  We use a large-scale production dataset, comprising over a year of customer interaction logs from a high-traffic e-commerce platform, to evaluate the scalability of several state-of-the-art architectures and their ensembles. Our key findings are: (1) selecting the right backbone and scaling factors is crucial; (2) the impact of scaling backbone, embedding, and data is largely independent and additive, which has implications for more efficient scaling exploration; (3) a streamlined warmstart strategy can accelerate training iterations while simplifying new updates; (4) inference optimization strategies such as decoupled graph execution and dynamic batching can enable low-latency GPU serving even for high-capacity models. Compared to a baseline of a pre-scaling production model, we ultimately deployed a model trained on 2.5x larger training data with 8x more inference compute while having minimal latency impact. Online A/B tests also demonstrate that our launches achieved a combined +2.6% gain in a key metric of search conversion rate.

### [118] [CrossAlpha: An Annual-Report Benchmark for Cross-Market Factor Research](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29286)
*Qian Wang,Zhongyi Tong,Nuo Chen,Zhaomin Wu,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文发布了首个跨市场金融NLP基准CrossAlpha，通过标准化异构披露文件并严格对齐交易时间，构建了包含3600家企业的全球企业关联图谱，证实了跨市场披露信息对预测股价收益的显著优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的公开基准缺乏对“跨市场披露到收益（Disclosure-to-Return）”这一评估维度的支持。由于不同市场间存在语言差异、监管标准不一、报告模板导致的披露偏见以及跨市场交易时间不对齐等挑战，量化研究难以有效地利用全球范围内的企业信息来预测收益。

Method: 该论文提出了CrossAlpha基准，包含三个核心组件：1. 披露蒸馏（Disclosure Distillation）：将多语言、多监管体系下的异构披露文件转化为标准化的十类英文业务描述；2. 残差模式图构建（Residual Schema Graph Construction）：利用主成分分析（PCA）白化技术处理披露模式得分，构建去偏的跨市场企业关联图；3. 时间对齐评估（Timing-Aligned Evaluation）：整合11年的日频交易数据，在严格的跨市场交易协议下进行回测与标签构建。

Result: CrossAlpha涵盖了美、日、台、韩、港5个市场的约3600家企业。实验表明，基于该基准构建的跨市场企业关联在预测性能上优于传统的行业代码和历史收益相关性基准。特别是在美日市场迁移实验中，其ICIR达到0.39（对比基准仅为0.07-0.18），证明了跨市场信号具备稳健的Alpha预测能力。

Conclusion: CrossAlpha 是一个开源且可复用的基准，填补了跨市场金融NLP研究的空白，证明了从企业披露信息中提取的跨市场信号具有显著的预测价值，为全球资本市场的多因子量化研究提供了重要的基础设施。

Abstract: Cross-market factor research studies whether firm-level signals from one or more markets can predict returns in a target market, but existing public benchmarks do not support cross-market disclosure-to-return evaluation. Building such a benchmark is challenging because filings differ across languages and regulatory systems, disclosure-derived similarity can be biased by common reporting components, and cross-market signals must be evaluated under feasible trading-time alignment. We introduce \textbf{CrossAlpha}, a public annual-report benchmark for cross-market factor research. CrossAlpha addresses these challenges through three corresponding components: \emph{Disclosure Distillation}, which standardises heterogeneous filings into ten-category English business descriptions; \emph{Residual Schema Graph Construction}, which builds PCA-whitened cross-market firm-pair scores from schema-level disclosures; and \emph{Timing-Aligned Evaluation}, which pairs the graph with 11 years of daily OHLCV data to construct forward-return labels under feasible cross-market execution protocols. CrossAlpha covers about 3,600 firms and 10,700 firm-year reports from the United States, Japan, Taiwan, South Korea, and Hong Kong, and releases about 19M directed firm-pair scores. In experiments, disclosure-derived cross-market peers outperform domestic text, industry-code, and return-correlation peers in the US-to-Japan setting (ICIR 0.39 versus 0.07--0.18), and cross-market sources beat the domestic text baseline in most target markets. CrossAlpha offers an open-sourced, reusable, return-grounded benchmark for cross-market financial NLP.

</details>


### [119] [UniNote: A Unified Embedding Model for Multimodal Representation and Ranking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29287)
*Jinghan Zhao,Wenwei Jin,Anqi Li,Jintao Tong,Luya Mo,Jiawei Li,Bin Li,Yao Hu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: UniNote是一种专为工业级I2I检索设计的统一嵌入模型，通过对比SFT与强化学习两阶段训练，并结合Matryoshka表示学习，实现了检索精度与系统效率的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态嵌入方法在工业级I2I检索场景中存在局限性，难以平衡全局表征与细粒度检索，且解码后的嵌入与排序流水线存在系统性低效，同时在模型精度与服务延迟之间难以取得理想的权衡。

Method: 1. 采用定制化检索策略处理复杂的多模态内容。2. 引入两阶段训练范式：第一阶段利用对比监督微调（Contrastive SFT）构建基础嵌入；第二阶段通过强化学习（RL）对齐内容相关性，优化排序质量。3. 结合Matryoshka表示学习（MRL）以提升检索质量并降低计算成本。

Result: UniNote在多项I2I检索任务中实现了SOTA性能。在小红书的部署实践表明，该模型显著提升了大规模应用中的检索质量，并有效降低了系统成本。

Conclusion: UniNote通过统一嵌入模型架构与两阶段训练范式，成功解决了工业级I2I检索中全局表征与细粒度检索平衡、系统效率及精度延迟权衡的问题，证明了其在实际大规模应用中的高效性与优越性。

Abstract: Item-to-Item (I2I) retrieval is a fundamental part of modern content platforms, supporting critical industrial workflows from recommendation engines to content auditing. While multimodal embedding methods have advanced general retrieval, they often falter in I2I scenarios due to the challenges of balancing global content representation with fine-grained local retrieval, the systemic inefficiency of decoupled embedding-and-ranking pipelines, and the inherent trade-offs between model precision and serving latency. To solve these issues, we propose \textbf{UniNote}, a unified embedding model designed for industrial I2I retrieval. Tailored retrieval strategies are introduced to support representation learning over complex, multimodal content at varying granularities. To operationalize these strategies, UniNote employs a two-stage training paradigm: the first stage leverages contrastive SFT to establish robust base embeddings, while the second stage refines ranking quality through a reinforcement learning (RL) process that aligns the model with content relevance. Our results show that UniNote achieves SOTA performance across diverse I2I tasks. Deployed at Xiaohongshu and integrated with Matryoshka Representation Learning (MRL), UniNote achieved significant improvements in retrieval quality and cost efficiency in large-scale applications.

</details>


### [120] [ACE: Anisotropy-Controllable Embedding for LLM-enhanced Sequential Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29322)
*Dongcheol Lee,Hye-young Kim,Jongwuk Lee*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM在序列推荐中生成嵌入各向异性严重的问题，提出了ACE方法。通过线性自编码器在维持语义的同时优化嵌入的几何分布，显著提升了推荐系统的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于LLM的提取器范式在序列推荐中展现潜力，但LLM生成的嵌入通常存在严重的各向异性（向量高度集中），导致模型在微调阶段难以有效吸收协作信号，限制了推荐性能。

Method: 提出了各向异性可控嵌入（ACE）方法，该方法利用线性自编码器（LAE）重塑嵌入分布，通过L2正则化控制维度离散度以缓解各向异性，并结合重构损失函数以确保原始语义结构的完整性。

Result: 实验结果显示，ACE显著优于现有的LLM增强序列推荐模型，在Recall@20和NDCG@20指标上分别取得了最高12.4%和11.8%的性能提升。

Conclusion: ACE通过显式控制LLM生成嵌入的各向异性，成功解决了其在序列推荐任务中的几何不平衡问题，实现了语义保留与几何分布均匀性之间的平衡，为增强序列推荐性能提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Recent advances in the LLM-as-Extractor paradigm leverage large language models (LLMs) to transfer semantically rich item embeddings into sequential recommendation (SR) backbones. However, LLM-generated embeddings often suffer from strong anisotropy. Most vectors are concentrated in similar directions, resulting in a geometric imbalance that makes it difficult to adapt to collaborative signals during fine-tuning. To address this challenge, we propose Anisotropy-Controllable Embedding (ACE), which explicitly controls the anisotropy of LLM-generated embeddings. Specifically, ACE utilizes a linear autoencoder (LAE) to reshape the embedding distribution while preserving its semantic structure. In this process, the L2-regularization term mitigates the anisotropy by controlling the dispersion of embedding dimensions, while the reconstruction loss maintains semantic relationships among items. That is, ACE balances geometric uniformity and semantic embedding preservation for more stable learning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ACE consistently outperforms existing LLM-enhanced SR models, yielding improvements of up to 12.4% and 11.8% in Recall@20 and NDCG@20, respectively.

</details>


### [121] [Latent Terms: Dense Retrievers Contain Trivially Extractable BM25-ready Zipfian Vocabularies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29384)
*Benjamin Clavié,Sean Lee,Aamir Shakir,Makoto P. Kato*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为“潜在项”（Latent Terms）的新方法，能够从现有的密集检索模型中无监督地提取出高质量的稀疏特征，从而在无需额外训练的情况下，利用传统BM25实现超越原模型性能的稀疏检索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管当前密集检索模型性能强大，但其内部表示往往被视为“黑盒”，且难以直观解释；研究者旨在探索密集检索模型中是否存在可利用的、能够转化为稀疏检索特征的内在结构，以提升检索的表达能力和可索引性。

Method: 提出了一种名为“潜在项”（Latent Terms）的方法，利用稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoders）对冻结的密集检索模型进行处理，将其表示分解为符合齐普夫定律（Zipfian）分布的稀疏词汇表，并利用传统的BM25评分函数进行检索。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在不需要额外稀疏检索监督的情况下，其检索表现能够匹敌甚至超过原基础模型的单向量评分方法以及现有的SPLADE变体，并在专门针对单向量检索缺陷设计的LIMIT数据集上表现出色。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了密集检索模型内部蕴含着可直接用于稀疏检索的丰富结构，通过稀疏自编码器提取这些“潜在项”（Latent Terms），无需专门的训练即可实现高性能的稀疏检索，打破了密集与稀疏检索方法的界限。

Abstract: We propose Latent Terms, a method revealing that models trained for dense retrieval, whether single- or multi-vector, learn representations that can trivially be decomposed into retrieval-ready sparse features. When trained on frozen retrievers, Sparse Autoencoders without any retrieval-specific adjustments extract a latent vocabulary with approximately Zipfian collection statistics, directly suitable for classical sparse retrieval scoring via BM25. This approach enables sparse retrieval while requiring no learned expansion objective or sparse retrieval supervision whatsoever, and can be readily applied to any dense retriever. Latent Terms is able to match or outperform single-vector scoring methods from its own base model as well as comparable SPLADE variants. In addition, it substantially outperforms its base model on LIMIT, a task specifically designed to highlight the failures of single-vector retrieval. Overall, our results highlight that neural retrievers contain more expressive and indexable structure than their default scoring functions expose, but that other methods can nonetheless be leveraged.

### [122] [FLASH-MAXSIM: IO-Aware Fused Kernels for Late-Interaction Scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29517)
*Roi Pony,Adi Raz Goldfarb,Idan Friedman,Daniel Ezer,Udi Barzelay*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Flash-MaxSim 提出了一种无需物化相似度张量的 GPU 融合计算方法，大幅降低了 ColBERT 等延迟交互检索模型的内存开销，并显著提升了计算速度，同时保持了原始检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的延迟交互（Late-interaction）检索模型（如 ColBERT、ColPali）在实现 MaxSim 操作时，需要物化一个巨大的查询-文档相似度张量，这导致极高的显存占用，限制了批处理大小（batch size），甚至在处理中等规模数据集时就会耗尽高端 GPU 的内存。

Method: 提出 Flash-MaxSim，一种 IO 感知型的 GPU 融合核函数。该方法通过将查询和文档分块（tiles）流式传输至片上 SRAM，直接在计算过程中完成最大相似度（MaxSim）的规约，无需物化中间相似度张量。此外，作者还引入了反向传播中的逆网格 CSR 构建、INT8 量化以及无填充（padding-free）的可变长度处理技术，进一步优化了内存和计算效率。

Result: 在 A100 GPU 上，Flash-MaxSim 的推理速度提升高达 3.9 倍（在 H100 上达 4.7 倍）；推理显存使用量减少至 1/16，训练显存使用量减少约 28 倍；同时保持了与 FP32 基准完全一致的排序性能（Top-20 一致率为 100%）。

Conclusion: Flash-MaxSim 通过 IO 感知型融合核函数技术，成功解决了延迟交互检索（如 ColBERT、ColPali）中张量显存占用过高的问题。该方法在不损失精度的前提下，实现了显著的内存节省和计算加速，为大规模检索模型的训练与推理提供了高效且可扩展的基础设施。

Abstract: Late-interaction retrieval (ColBERT, ColPali) scores a query against a document with the MaxSim operator: for every query token, the maximum similarity over the document tokens, summed over
  query tokens. The standard implementation materializes the full query-token x document-token similarity tensor in GPU memory; for visual ColPali at 10K documents this tensor alone is 21 GB in
  FP16, created only to be reduced to one score per document and discarded. It exhausts a 40 GB GPU and bounds the achievable batch size in both inference and training. We present
  Flash-MaxSim, an IO-aware fused GPU kernel that computes exactly the same scores without ever materializing the tensor, by streaming query and document tiles through on-chip SRAM and folding
  the row-maximum reduction into the same pass. We extend the IO-aware principle through the training backward pass, an inverse-grid CSR construction that reuses the forward argmax for an
  atomic-free, destination-owned gradient reduction, and through INT8xINT8 quantization and variable-length (padding-free) scoring. Flash-MaxSim is up to 3.9x faster on an A100 (4.7x on an
  H100) than naive PyTorch at matched precision, uses up to 16x less inference memory and ~28x less training memory, unlocks corpus and batch sizes that exhaust PyTorch entirely, preserves the
  exact ranking (100% top-20 agreement with an FP32 reference)

</details>


### [123] [Rec-Distill: An Industrial Distillation Pipeline for Large-Scale Recommendation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29755)
*Haoran Ding,Wenlin Zhao,Yuchen Jiang,Juren Li,Jie Zhu,Xinchun Li,Yishujie Zhao,Yi Zhang,Ao Qiao,Jianhui Dong,Cheng Chen,Ziyan Gong,Deping Xie,Peng Xu,Zikai Wang,Yuwei Wang,Huizhi Yang,Zhe Chen,Yuchao Zheng*

TL;DR: Rec-Distill 是一种工业级推荐系统蒸馏框架，通过一系列技术优化，将超大规模推荐模型的性能高效迁移至轻量化线上部署模型，解决了大规模模型落地难的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模推荐模型虽性能优越，但因工业环境对计算效率和延迟的严苛要求，难以直接部署，导致离线性能提升与在线业务落地之间存在显著差距。

Method: 提出了名为 Rec-Distill 的工业蒸馏流水线，核心技术包括：大规模教师模型扩展、学生端解耦训练、黑盒蒸馏策略、去偏机制以及适应动态推荐环境的混合批流处理流程。

Result: 该框架成功将教师模型扩展至 240 亿稠密参数及 2 万行为序列长度，同时使轻量化学生模型恢复了超过 60% 的教师性能提升，并在多个真实推荐与广告场景中实现了显著的业务指标增长。

Conclusion: Rec-Distill 提供了一个有效的工业级解决方案，成功桥接了离线大规模推荐模型与在线轻量化部署之间的鸿沟，证明了通过知识蒸馏将大规模模型收益迁移至生产环境的可行性与商业价值。

Abstract: Large recommendation models have demonstrated substantial potential gains under scaling laws, yet these gains are difficult to realize in industrial recommendation systems because real-world deployment requires lightweight models with strict serving efficiency and latency guarantees. This creates a fundamental gap between offline model scaling and online deployment. In this work, we present Rec-Distill, an industrial distillation pipeline that transfers the performance gains of large-scale recommendation modeling to efficient serving models. Rec-Distill combines large-teacher scaling with student-side transfer optimization through decoupled training, black-box distillation, debiasing mechanism, and a hybrid batch-streaming pipeline for dynamic recommendation environments. Across multiple recommendation and advertising scenarios on real-world platforms, our framework scales teacher models up to 24B dense parameters and 20K behavior sequence length, while enabling lightweight students to recover a substantial portion of teacher gains, with distillation transferability exceeding 60% in the best setting. Extensive offline and online experiments further show that these transferred gains consistently translate into measurable business improvements under industrial constraints. These results demonstrate that Rec-Distill provides a practical framework for distilling large-scale recommendation models into deployable, cost-efficient serving systems, while also establishing a reliable path toward scaling recommendation models to even larger regimes in the future.

### [124] [Uncertainty Quantification for Multimodal Retrieval Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29956)
*Simon Binz,Heydar Soudani,Faegheh Hasibi*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对多模态RAG系统中不确定性难以量化的问题，提出了LeMUQ方法，通过分析输入修改下的token概率交互，显著提升了模型对输出可靠性的评估准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的不确定性量化（UQ）方法主要针对文本模型，无法有效解决多模态检索增强生成（Multimodal RAG）中因检索、视觉理解及生成阶段产生的复杂不确定性，导致生成结果可能出现错误或误导。

Method: 提出了LeMUQ（Learnable Multimodal UQ）方法。该方法通过输入修改（如移除模态或检索到的上下文）来分析token概率，将这些信号编码为“概率token”，并利用微调模型处理这些信号，从而捕捉模态与检索之间的交互作用。

Result: 在多个数据集、检索器和视觉语言模型（VLM）上的实验表明，LeMUQ的AUROC指标平均提升了3.8%，且在不同检索设置和数据集上表现出较强的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 通过对多模态及检索感知概率信号进行建模，LeMUQ有效提升了多模态RAG系统的不确定性量化能力，为构建更可靠、更安全的系统提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Retrieval Augmented Generation (RAG) improves the question answering capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) by incorporating external knowledge and has recently been extended to multimodal settings through Vision-Language Models (VLMs) that integrate visual and textual information. Despite these advances, generated answers can still be incorrect or misleading. Uncertainty Quantification (UQ) methods aim to estimate the reliability of model outputs, but most existing approaches are designed for text-only models and perform poorly in multimodal RAG scenarios. A key challenge is capturing uncertainty arising from multiple stages of the pipeline, including retrieval, visual understanding, and generation. In this work, we show that modeling uncertainty using multimodal and retrieval-aware probability signals improves estimation in multimodal RAG systems. We introduce LeMUQ, a Learnable Multimodal UQ method that analyzes token probabilities under input modifications, such as removing modalities or retrieved context. By encoding these signals as probability tokens and processing them with a finetuned model, our approach captures interactions between modalities and retrieval. Experiments across datasets, retrievers, and VLMs show consistent improvements over baseline and finetuned UQ methods. Our proposed LeMUQ increases the AUROC metric by 3.8% on average. Additionally, our method shows strong generalization performance across different retrieval setups and datasets with mixed results when transferring across different VLMs. Our findings highlight the importance of modeling multimodal uncertainty and provide a step toward more reliable and safer multimodal RAG systems. Code is available on GitHub.

### [125] [No More K-means:Single-Stage Sparse Coding for Efficient Multi-Vector Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30120)
*Lixuan Guo,Yifei Wang,Tiansheng Wen,Aosong Feng,Stefanie Jegelka,Chenyu You*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种单阶段稀疏检索（SSR）方法，利用稀疏自编码器将词元嵌入转化为高维稀疏表示，替代了低效的向量聚类，在显著提升索引构建速度和检索效率的同时，实现了检索准确率的提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多向量检索模型（如ColBERT）在处理大规模语料时，因词元级特征存储与计算压力巨大，被迫依赖降维和聚类，这不仅导致了索引构建的延迟，还造成了关键语义信息的损失。因此需要一种更高效的替代方案。

Method: 提出单阶段稀疏检索（SSR）框架。该方法放弃了传统多向量检索中的K-means聚类与压缩机制，转而利用稀疏自编码器（SAE）将词元嵌入投影为高维、高度稀疏的表示，并结合倒排索引技术实现高效检索。

Result: 在BEIR基准测试中，SSR相较于ColBERTv2索引速度提升了15倍，检索延迟降低了一半，且在检索性能指标上优于主流基线模型。

Conclusion: SSR通过稀疏自编码器成功实现了多向量检索范式的升级，证明了在保留精细化语义的同时，可以通过高效的倒排索引解决计算与存储的瓶颈，为大规模检索系统提供了更优的平衡方案。

Abstract: Multi-vector retrieval (MVR) models, exemplified by ColBERT, have established new benchmarks in retrieval accuracy by preserving fine-grained token-level interactions. However, this granularity imposes prohibitive storage and retrieval efficiency bottlenecks: to manage the immense memory footprint and computational overhead of billion-scale token vectors, state-of-the-art systems are forced to rely on aggressive dimension reduction and complex clustering (e.g., K-means). This compromise introduces two critical limitations: excessive indexing latency of clustering large-scale corpora and semantic information loss inherent to compression. In this paper, we propose Single-stage Sparse Retrieval (SSR}, a paradigm shift that replaces expensive clustering with efficient sparse coding. Instead of compressing features into low-dimensional dense vectors, we utilize Sparse Autoencoder (SAE) to project token embeddings into a high-dimensional but highly sparse representation. This transformation enables us to bypass vector clustering entirely and leverage inverted indexing for precise, high-throughput retrieval. Extensive experiments on the BEIR benchmark demonstrate that SSR achieves a "trifecta" of improvements: it reduces indexing time by 15x compared to ColBERTv2, halves retrieval latency, and simultaneously improves retrieval performance over leading baselines.

### [126] [LexPath: A domain-oriented multi-path framework for legal article retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30205)
*Weixuan Liu,Qingfeng Zhuge,Xuyang Chen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对法律领域检索中语义与法律逻辑脱节的问题，LexPath 通过融合 IRAC 逻辑与法律结构信息的双路径检索及意图重排序机制，实现了更精准的法律条款匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的通用领域检索方法过分依赖文本表层语义或词法相似度，难以区分在文本上相似但在法律适用上不相关的条款，无法满足构建可追溯、可靠法律 AI 系统对精确匹配的需求。

Method: 提出 LexPath 框架，包含两个核心模块：1. 多路径检索模块：结合 IRAC（事实-规则-分析-结论）导向的稀疏路径（关键词扩展）和结构导向的密集路径（利用法律层级与引用关系进行硬负样本训练）；2. 意图感知重排序模块：通过计算查询与法律条款之间的意图一致性分数，对初步检索结果进行精炼。

Result: 在两个公开基准数据集以及一个自建的专业领域基准数据集上进行了测试，实验结果表明 LexPath 在检索准确性上显著优于现有的词法检索、密集检索、混合检索以及自适应 RAG 基准模型。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 LexPath 框架通过结合多路径检索与意图感知重排序技术，有效解决了法律条款检索中“文本相似但法律适用性低”的问题，为构建可追溯、可靠的法律 AI 系统提供了有效方案。

Abstract: Legal article retrieval is critical for building traceable and reliable legal AI systems, where conclusions must be grounded in specific legal articles. However, existing open-domain retrieval methods rely heavily on surface-level lexical or semantic similarity, making it difficult for them to distinguish legally relevant articles from those that are textually similar but legally inapplicable or misaligned with the user's underlying intent. To bridge this gap, we propose \textsc{LexPath}, a domain-oriented multi-path framework comprising a multi-path retrieval module and an intent-aware reranking module. The retrieval module combines two complementary legal-specific paths to collect candidate articles: an IRAC-guided sparse path that expands queries with legally informative keywords, and a structure-guided dense path trained with hard negatives derived from legal hierarchy and citation relations. Then, the reranking module further refines the candidate ranking by incorporating the intent consistency score between queries and legal articles. We evaluate \textsc{LexPath} on two publicly available benchmarks focusing on general-public queries and a self-constructed benchmark targeting domain-professional scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate that \textsc{LexPath} consistently outperforms lexical, dense, hybrid, and adaptive retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) baselines. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of each component.

### [127] [GRASP: Plan-Guided Graph Retrieval with Adaptive Fusion and Reranking on Semi-Structured Knowledge Bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30237)
*Yicheng Tao,Yiqun Wang,Xiangchen Song,Xin Luo,Kai Liu,Jie Liu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 GRASP 的三阶段 SKB 检索框架，通过融合计划驱动的图检索、计划条件式文本检索和精调重排序，显著提升了半结构化知识库的检索性能，在 STaRK 基准测试中取得了显著的性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的半结构化知识库（SKB）检索系统在处理文本与结构化数据的融合时存在局限性，通常仅使用图进行简单的查询扩展，或者采用简单的全局加权方法，难以充分利用知识库的丰富语义和结构信息，因此需要一种更高效的统一检索框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GRASP 的三阶段检索框架：1) 基于计划的图检索（Plan-based Graph Retrieval），从结构化数据中提取相关路径；2) 计划条件融合（Plan-conditioned Fusion），将检索到的图结构信息与稠密文本检索器（Dense Retriever）的结果进行深度融合；3) 精调重排序（Fine-tuned Reranker），对融合后的候选集进行最终的排序优化。

Result: 在 STaRK 基准测试中，GRASP 在所有评估指标上均大幅超越现有最优方法，将平均 Hit@1 指标从 62.0% 提升至 73.9%。消融实验和敏感性分析进一步验证了该框架各模块的有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: GRASP 框架通过结合计划驱动的图检索、计划条件融合以及精调的重排序模型，有效地解决了半结构化知识库（SKB）检索中的异构数据融合难题，显著提升了检索准确率，为未来知识库检索系统提供了一种鲁棒且高效的新范式。

Abstract: Semi-structured knowledge bases (SKBs) embed textual documents in a typed graph of entities and relations, and underpin applications such as product search, academic paper search, and precision-medicine inquiries. Existing hybrid retrieval systems on SKBs either use the graph only for query expansion, mix textual and structural branches under a global weighting, or rely on fine-tuned graph-traversal generators. We present GRASP, a three-stage SKB retrieval framework unifying plan-based graph retrieval, plan-conditioned fusion with a dense retriever, and a fine-tuned reranker over the fused candidates. GRASP substantially advances the state of the art on every metric across the three STaRK benchmarks, lifting average Hit@1 from 62.0 to 73.9. Ablation and sensitivity studies further confirm the effectiveness and robustness of GRASP.

### [128] [Behavior-Induced Mirror-Prox Temporal-Difference Learning for Faster Off-Policy Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28849)
*Xingguo Chen,Yuchen Shen,Shangdong Yang,Chao Li,Guang Yang,Wenhao Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种改进的离策略预测方法 STHTD-MP，通过将行为策略的 Bellman 矩阵引入度量空间来改善梯度 TD 方法的几何特性，从而实现更优的收敛性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的梯度时间差分（Gradient TD）方法在离策略预测中受限于辅助变量度量带来的几何影响，通常使用的特征协方差度量可能不是最优的。研究人员希望利用行为策略的转换信息，构建一种更具信息量的更新几何结构，以提高学习算法的稳定性和效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为 STHTD-MP 的行为引导型 Mirror-Prox 时间差分学习方法。该方法将原始-对偶鞍点公式中的协方差度量替换为行为策略 Bellman 矩阵的对称部分，并采用 Mirror-Prox 预测-校正步骤进行更新，同时对该算法在固定策略线性预测下的收敛性进行了形式化证明。

Result: 理论分析证明了该算法在标准随机近似假设下收敛；误差边界和平均算子比较表明，在行为诱导度量优化了几何结构时，STHTD-MP 的平均收缩因子优于 GTD2-MP；在多项基准测试（Random Walk, Boyan Chain 等）中的数值分析验证了其优越性，并分析了 Baird 反例作为奇异边界情况的表现。

Conclusion: STHTD-MP 通过利用行为策略的 Bellman 矩阵作为度量，有效地改善了鞍点问题的几何结构，在理论和实验上证明了其在某些任务中比传统的 GTD2-MP 方法具有更快的收敛性能和更小的平均收缩因子，同时也指出了该方法在特定极端情况下的局限性。

Abstract: Gradient temporal-difference methods provide stable off-policy prediction with linear function approximation, but their practical performance is strongly affected by the geometry induced by the auxiliary-variable metric. Existing Mirror-Prox TD methods typically use the feature covariance metric, whereas hybrid TD methods suggest that behavior-policy transition information can provide a more informative update geometry. This paper proposes a behavior-induced Mirror-Prox temporal-difference method, called STHTD-MP, which replaces the covariance metric in the primal-dual saddle-point formulation with the symmetric part of the behavior-policy Bellman matrix. The method keeps a single learning rate for the primal and auxiliary variables and applies a Mirror-Prox prediction-correction step to the resulting hybrid saddle-point operator. We provide a formal convergence analysis for fixed-policy linear prediction under standard stochastic approximation assumptions: the behavior-induced metric is positive definite, the joint mean system is Hurwitz, boundedness follows from a Lyapunov argument, and the stochastic recursion converges by the ODE method. We further derive projected-oracle ergodic gap bounds and an exact mean-operator comparison with GTD2-MP based on the spectral radius of the deterministic Mirror-Prox error matrix. The analysis shows that STHTD-MP can have a smaller mean contraction factor than GTD2-MP when the behavior-induced metric improves the saddle-point geometry. Exact numerical mean-operator analysis on two-state, Random Walk, and Boyan Chain benchmarks supports this condition, while Baird's counterexample is identified as a singular boundary case where the strict assumptions fail.

</details>


### [129] [The Cognitive Categorical Transformer: Category-Theoretic Inductive Biases for Language Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28864)
*Al Kari*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过在GPT-2 Small架构中集成范畴论驱动的“单纯形消息传递”模块，在保持训练协议一致的情况下，显著提升了语言模型的预测性能，并揭示了结构化先验对模型性能提升的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索将范畴论（Category Theory）中的数学结构与认知科学原理融入大语言模型架构中，是否能够超越传统Transformer架构，进一步提升语言建模的性能。

Method: 基于GPT-2 Small骨干网，构建了包含3.06亿参数的认知范畴Transformer（CCT）。引入了基于范畴论的“单纯形消息传递”（GT-Full）机制，并结合认知科学的启发进行组件设计。在WikiText-103数据集上通过匹配步数协议与基准模型进行对比，并进行了消融实验以验证各模块贡献。

Result: CCT模型在WikiText-103上的验证困惑度（PPL）达到21.27，相较于同等训练配置的GPT-2 Small（24.19 PPL）降低了2.92点（约12%）。消融实验表明，其中84%的性能提升归功于“单纯形消息传递”（GT-Full）模块。

Conclusion: 本文提出了“结构/一致性区别”（structure/consistency distinction）这一经验模式：引入新拓扑结构的范畴先验（如GT-Full）能有效提升语言模型性能，而强制执行一致性恒等式的先验则无效。该研究为将范畴论和认知科学引入深度学习架构提供了实证支持。

Abstract: The Cognitive Categorical Transformer (CCT) is a 306M-parameter architecture that augments a pretrained GPT-2 Small backbone with cognitively grounded components derived from category theory and several inspirations from cognitive science. Under a matched-step protocol (215,000 optimizer steps, matched data, matched optimizer and schedule) on WikiText-103, CCT reaches 21.27 validation perplexity, compared with 24.19 for an identically fine-tuned GPT-2 Small baseline. The architecture therefore contributes a 2.92 PPL (12% relative) reduction beyond what in-domain fine-tuning alone provides. A retrain-from-scratch ablation that holds GT-Full simplicial message passing bypassed across the entire seven-phase activation schedule reaches 23.72 PPL, localizing 84% of the architectural improvement (2.45 of 2.92 PPL) to GT-Full. We present the first ablation-validated evidence that simplicial message passing improves language-model perplexity at the 306M-parameter scale on WikiText-103. Published GPT-2 Large reaches 22.05 zero-shot PPL on WikiText-103 with 6.2x more parameters than GPT-2 Small; this paper treats that number as an external published reference, not as the architectural benchmark. Three negative results on consistency-style categorical priors (sheaf smoothing, adjunction round-trip, curvature regularization) and the joint structural-prior result for GT-Full and PrecisionWeightedPP together support an empirical pattern termed the *structure/consistency distinction*, in which categorical priors that add new topology improve language modeling and those that enforce a consistency identity do not.

### [130] [Review Arcade: On the Human Alignment and Gameability of LLM Reviews](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28897)
*Hans Ole Hatzel,Sebastian Steindl,Jan Strich*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该研究利用 2025 年 ACL Rolling Review (ARR) 的论文数据进行实证分析。方法包括：1. 评估 LLM 生成评审与人类专家评审之间的一致性；2. 测试不同提示词（Prompts）和模型（Models）对评审质量及一致性的影响；3. 构建作者利用 LLM 进行“迭代修改-重新评审”的模拟工作流，评估该流程对论文评分的潜在影响。

Result: 1. LLM 评审与人类评审之间仅存在有限的一致性，且在不同模型和提示词设置下表现差异巨大。2. 实验表明，作者利用 LLM 辅助进行“迭代修改-再评审”的工作流是有效的，在特定场景下可使高达 35% 的论文获得统计学意义上的评分提升。

Conclusion: LLM 在同行评审中的应用存在显著的不确定性。虽然 LLM 评审与人类评审之间存在一定程度的一致性，但这种一致性高度依赖于提示词和模型选择。此外，通过迭代修改“刷分”行为在某些情况下确实能提升论文评分，这引发了关于科研诚信和评审机制公正性的深层担忧，提示学术界需要重新审视 LLM 辅助评审的影响。

Abstract: LLM-generated reviews for scientific papers are gaining considerable traction and are even being officially piloted by major conferences. We have to assume that not only reviewers are using LLM-assistance, but also that authors use LLMs to revise their papers before submitting. In this work, we perform empirical experiments on papers from the 2025 ACL Rolling Review (ARR) to evaluate LLM reviews from both the author and the reviewer perspective. First, we identify a limited alignment of LLM reviews with human ones. In the best-case scenario, the alignment is reasonable. However, we also find that LLM-human alignment varies substantially across prompts and models. Finally, we investigate the scenario in which the author uses an iterative draft-revise workflow to improve the submission according to the LLM review. We find that this "gaming" of LLM reviews can be effective in specific scenarios, leading to a statistically significant increase of overall scores for up to 35\% of papers. We publish our code: https://github.com/uhh-hcds/reviewarcade.

### [131] [Orthogonal Concept Erasure for Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28902)
*Yuhao Sun,Lingyun Yu,Haoxiang Xu,Fengyuan Miao,Zhuoer Xu,Hongtao Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为正交概念擦除（OCE）的新型编辑式方法，通过几何视角的乘法参数更新取代了传统的加法更新，实现了对扩散模型中特定概念的高效、精确擦除，同时解决了生成能力退化的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型概念擦除方法存在局限：训练方法计算代价高，而编辑方法（基于加法参数更新）会导致概念擦除与生成能力保持之间的纠缠，难以同时实现精确擦除和性能保留。研究发现概念语义依赖于神经元方向，而生成能力依赖于角度几何，加法更新干扰了这些属性。

Method: 提出正交概念擦除（OCE）方法。该方法将编辑式擦除重构为乘法参数更新，通过推导出的闭式解，应用逐层正交变换来擦除概念，同时保持神经元幅度和角度几何结构不变。针对多概念擦除冲突问题，OCE 引入了基于子空间结构的操纵目标。

Result: 实验表明，OCE 在单概念和多概念擦除任务中均优于现有方法，能有效擦除目标概念并保护非目标内容，且表现出极高的效率，可在 4.3 秒内完成多达 100 个概念的擦除。

Conclusion: OCE 通过引入几何视角下的乘法参数更新机制，成功解决了编辑式概念擦除方法中参数更新带来的干扰问题，在实现高效、精确的概念擦除的同时，最大限度地保留了模型的生成性能，是当前概念擦除领域的一种高效且稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Concept erasure has emerged as a promising approach to mitigate undesired or unsafe content in diffusion models, yet existing methods still face significant limitations. While training-based methods are effective, their high computational cost limits scalability. Editing-based methods are more efficient and deployment-friendly, yet they struggle to simultaneously achieve precise concept erasure and preserve overall generative capacity. We identify this core limitation of the editing-based methods as reliance on additive parameter updates. Our empirical analysis reveals that concept semantics primarily depend on neuron direction rather than neuron magnitude, while overall generative capacity relies on the angular geometry of neurons. As additive updates inherently entangle direction, magnitude, and angular geometry, they inevitably introduce unintended interference between concept erasure and overall generation performance. To address this, we propose Orthogonal Concept Erasure (OCE), which reformulates editing-based erasure as multiplicative parameter updates from a geometric perspective. Specifically, OCE applies layer-wise orthogonal transformations derived from a closed-form solution to the parameters, enabling precise concept erasure while preserving the neuron magnitude and angular geometry. Furthermore, to address conflicting constraints in multi-concept erasure, OCE introduces a subspace-level objective with structured subspace manipulation, yielding a more effective and scalable erasure. Extensive experiments on single- and multi-concept erasure demonstrate that OCE outperforms existing methods in concept erasure and non-target preservation, erasing up to 100 concepts in 4.3 s. Code: https://github.com/HansSunY/OCE.

</details>

Abstract: Finite Element Analysis (FEA) serves as the cornerstone of modern engineering design. However, its workflow is inherently complex and relies heavily on domain expertise. Although recent efforts have integrated Large Language Models (LLMs) into FEA, existing approaches face limitations in handling multimodal inputs and executing complex tasks. To address these limitations, we propose VFEAgent, an end-to-end multi-agent system designed to automate FEA modeling and simulation directly from input images and problem descriptions. Our methodology integrates two core components: (1) a multimodal vision-language multi-agent pipeline that employs ReAct-driven reasoning to extract structured FEA specifications from heterogeneous inputs and (2) a verification-first code synthesis framework, incorporating robust self-debugging and fallback mechanisms to ensure executability and physical validity. We systematically evaluated the system across various engineering mechanics scenarios. The results demonstrate that VFEAgent achieves a high success rate in generating complete and physically valid simulations, outperforming LLM-based baseline methods in reliability and correctness. These findings validate the feasibility of automating the complete FEA workflow, highlighting the framework's potential to liberate engineers from tedious manual analysis.

Abstract: AI tools to support real world decision making must be able to build simulation models that inform their recommendations and render them interpretable. The BEAMS Initiative aims to guide the development of AI tools for modeling and simulation toward forms that are responsible and ethical by establishing benchmarks for human centered modeling and simulation practices. The initiative uses open digital and organizational infrastructure to collaboratively evaluate AI tools for modeling and simulation. The open source sd ai project hosted by the initiative establishes transparency and enables contributions to be shared broadly. A steering group focuses on prioritizing potential benchmarks, while a technical group focuses on implementing the benchmarks in the form of automated tests. Tests for several distinct categories of evaluation have been implemented and applied to AI tools that support qualitative model building, quantitative model building, and model discussion. When engines from the sd ai project are coupled with different LLMs, their performance on these evaluations reveals variability across different AI tools. The evaluations implemented by the initiative demonstrate that AI enabled modeling tools perform better at discussion and basic qualitative tasks than with causal reasoning and quantitative error fixing. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Although a growing body of research has begun to describe user--LLM interactions, the picture it paints is largely static; little is known about how individual users change their behavior over time. To address this gap, we analyze the conversational trajectories of $\sim$12,000 randomly sampled Microsoft Bing Copilot users and compare these with data from WildChat-4.8M. While the Copilot data contains significant population-level trends, we find that trends in individual user trajectories are much weaker; user habits prove to be overwhelmingly sticky. We also find stark differences between users of different activity levels: more active users have more successful conversations and use the LLM for more complex and professionally oriented tasks. Some user trends also appear in WildChat-4.8M, but we find evidence that this dataset is significantly skewed towards highly proficient "power" users. Ultimately, our results suggest that existing user behavior is difficult to change and demonstrate the extent of user heterogeneity. Our comparison between datasets highlights that WildChat does not represent typical user-AI interactions, an important caveat for downstream uses of the data.

### [135] [When Models Disagree: Rethinking LLM Evaluation for Public Comment Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29025)
*Aisha Najera,Alvin Moon,Vedant Srinivasan,Rajesh Veeraraghavan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种通过检测大语言模型间分类分歧来评估公共政策评论的方法，指出仅靠准确率指标不足以衡量模型在复杂诠释性任务中的表现，并建议将“模型分歧”作为引导人工精准审核的核心诊断依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦机构在利用大语言模型（LLM）对公共评论语料库进行分类时，模型分类方式会直接影响政策制定者的决策视角及议题的优先级。目前的评估标准仅侧重于在小规模验证集上的立场准确性，无法检测不同模型在处理相同公共输入时产生的实质性诠释差异。

Method: 提出了“诠释性审计流程”（Interpretive Audit Pipeline）。该方法将多个LLM对同一输入产生的分类分歧作为诊断指标，识别出具有诠释复杂性的数据点，从而精准引导人工审核资源。研究通过对USDA docket的1,260条公共评论进行跨模型对比分析，并实施了包含初始标注、交叉查看他人标注、再次修订的“两阶段标注研究”来评估模型表现。

Result: 研究发现，不同模型间的主题分歧程度远高于同一模型在不同Prompt下的波动。专家标注规则虽然能压制表层的意见分歧，但无法从本质上解决深层的诠释矛盾。此外，在两阶段标注中发现，人类标注者的修订行为往往引入了模型群体共识之外的新框架，证明了现有模型在处理高度主观性文本时存在局限。

Conclusion: 基于分歧的评估方法是现有准确率指标的必要补充。在处理公共政策等复杂诠释性任务时，模型间的分歧反映了输入文本的固有复杂性，而非简单的错误。研究表明，单纯依赖专家规则并不能消除深层的诠释差异，必须引入人类的审慎介入。

Abstract: Federal agencies are deploying large language models (LLMs) to categorize public comment corpora, where the model's organization of the record shapes what policymakers see and which arguments register. Standard evaluation, anchored on stance accuracy against a small validated set, cannot detect when different models produce materially different categorizations of the same public input. We propose an Interpretive Audit Pipeline that treats multi-model disagreement as diagnostic of interpretive complexity and directs human review toward genuinely ambiguous public input. Analyzing 1,260 public comments on a federal USDA docket across four LLMs, we find that inter-model thematic divergence exceeds within-model prompt variation, and that an expert rubric suppresses deep interpretive disagreement without resolving it. In a two-stage labeling study on a stratified 40-comment subsample, four LLMs and a human annotator labeled independently and then revised after seeing the others' labels. Revision behavior varied across labelers, and the human annotator's revisions frequently introduced framings absent from the ensemble's collective output. We argue disagreement-based evaluation is a necessary complement to accuracy metrics for LLM-assisted interpretive coding.

### [136] [Mind Your Tone: Does Tone Alter LLM Performance?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29027)
*Om Dobariya,Akhil Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了提示词语调对大型语言模型回答客观题准确率的显著影响。实验发现不同模型对语调的敏感度存在巨大差异，提示开发者在部署应用时需警惕语调带来的性能波动，不可忽视提示词风格对模型可靠性的潜在干扰。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）的广泛应用，研究人员观察到其性能受到提示词风格和语调的影响。本文旨在深入探究提示词中的语调变化是否以及如何导致模型在处理客观选择题时产生准确率差异，从而揭示 LLM 在语调方面的敏感性问题。

Method: 研究团队构建了两个数据集：包含50个基础问题（5种语调变体）和570个MMLU子集问题（7种语调变体）。通过测试四种主流轻量级模型（GPT-4o, GPT-5-nano, Gemini 2.5 Flash, Gemini 2.5 Flash Lite），评估不同语调对模型回答客观选择题准确率的影响，并提出了一种路由框架来解释语调如何调节模型的内部推理模式。

Result: 实验表明，语调对不同模型的影响具有系统性，但程度差异巨大。部分模型表现出轻微但具有统计学意义的波动，而另一些模型则出现了显著的准确率浮动。此外，研究还发现了不同学科领域对语调敏感度的差异，并证实了语调确实能通过某种路由机制影响模型的内部推理过程。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型的表现并不具备“语调鲁棒性”。研究发现，提示词中的语调会对模型准确率产生系统性且具有模型差异性的影响。开发者在部署 LLM 应用时，必须考虑到提示词语调带来的潜在性能偏差，不能默认模型在不同语气下保持一致的可靠性。

Abstract: The use of Large Language Models (LLMs) is proliferating, yet their performance is observed to vary based on prompting styles and tones. In this study, we investigate both whether and how tonal variations in prompts lead to disparate LLM accuracy for objective multiple-choice questions. We use two datasets: a 50-base question dataset with five tone variants and a 570-base question MMLU subset spanning 57 subjects with seven tone variants. Experiments were conducted to evaluate the performance of four cost-efficient, popular LLMs: ChatGPT-4o, ChatGPT-5-nano, Gemini 2.5 Flash, and Gemini 2.5 Flash Lite. Across models, tonal effects are systematic but highly model-dependent. Some models show small, yet statistically significant, shifts, while others exhibit large accuracy swings across tones. Further, we identify subject-level differences in tone sensitivity and present a routing framework to explain how tones may attune internal reasoning modes. Our findings caution users against assuming tone-robust reliability in LLM deployments.

</details>

Abstract: This study reports findings from a cross-sectional survey (n = 72) of higher education practitioners examining beliefs, behaviors, and institutional conditions related to artificial intelligence (AI) integration in teaching and learning. Grounded in the DOT Framework, which integrates design thinking and open systems theory, the study investigates AI familiarity, usage patterns, design-oriented practices, and pedagogical beliefs. Exploratory factor analysis of 19 belief items identified a three-factor structure: AI Functional Capabilities, Oversight and Governance, and Instructor Collaboration and Planning (α = .90). Results indicate that practitioners hold favorable views of AI as a pedagogical support while maintaining strong commitments to human oversight and critical evaluation. Reported practices emphasize iterative prompting and content generation, with less consistent use of needs assessment and feedback loops. Institutional barriers including limited policy, training, and infrastructure were widely reported. These findings provide preliminary empirical support for the DOT Framework as a descriptive model of practitioner beliefs and practices, while also highlighting gaps between design-oriented theory and current implementation. The study contributes an initial measurement structure and identifies directions for confirmatory validation and outcome-based research linking AI-supported design practices to instructional quality.

### [138] [Rethinking Literature Search Evaluation: Deep Research Helps, and Human Citation Lists Are Not a Ground Truth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29234)
*Gaurav Sahu,Laurent Charlin,Christopher Pal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种通过广度优先搜索扩展的深度检索流水线，大幅提升了文献检索的召回率，并揭示了传统人类参考列表在评估中存在社交偏见与相关性不足的缺陷，主张采用多维度综合指标体系进行文献检索评价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大规模文献检索面临两方面问题：一是传统检索流水线效率不足，召回率低；二是现有评估基准（以人类参考列表为金标准）存在主观偏差及局限性。

Method: 1. 构建“深度研究”流水线：处理完整查询论文，并基于参考文献进行广度优先搜索以扩展检索结果。
2. 引入中立大模型（LLM-as-a-judge）作为评估工具，对比人类标注与AI生成的检索结果。
3. 利用OpenAlex合著者图谱，分析引用行为中的社交偏好（如合作者偏向）。

Result: 1. 新的检索流水线显著提升了检索能力，在RollingEval-Jun25基准上将召回率从20%以下提升至80%以上。
2. 研究发现人类参考列表存在局限，仅51%被判定为中等相关，而最优AI重排序器的相关度高达86-88%。
3. 发现人类倾向于引用自己的合作者，其频率是AI模型的2.5倍。

Conclusion: 文献检索评价不应仅依赖单一指标。研究强调应综合考量召回率、主题相关性得分、排序列表多样性以及合著者距离诊断，从而多维度衡量引用质量。

Abstract: We study large-scale literature search from two complementary angles: improving the retrieval pipeline, and stress-testing the human reference list as an evaluation target. First, we implement a Deep Research pipeline that processes the full query paper and expands the retrieved results breadth-first along their bibliographies, and show that it substantially outperforms vanilla API-only search, raising recall on RollingEval-Jun25 (a 250-paper literature-search benchmark) from below 20% to above 80%. Second, we use a neutral LLM-as-a-judge to determine if human references are sound ground truth for the task. We find significant limitations: only 51% of human citations are judged moderately relevant or higher, against 86--88% for the strongest AI-based re-rankers. We study this gap on the OpenAlex co-authorship graph, finding that humans are 2.5x more likely than the best AI re-rankers to cite a direct collaborator. Together, our results argue against single-axis literature-search evaluation: recall, topical-relevance scoring, ranked-list diversity, and a co-authorship-distance diagnostic each measure complementary properties of citation quality and should be reported jointly.

### [139] [Differentiable Belief-based Opponent Shaping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29042)
*Aarav G Sane,Karthik Sivachandran,Rohan Paleja*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 D-BOS 方法，通过对观察者的信念动态进行微分，使智能体能够通过影响他人的信念来优化自身的策略，从而在多智能体协作及隐藏角色游戏中取得了优异表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对手塑形方法多局限于参数或策略空间，而针对隐藏角色游戏的信念操纵技术往往依赖硬编码目标（如欺骗），缺乏灵活性。研究人员旨在开发一种能够通过环境奖励结构自然涌现出最优策略的方法，以通过影响他人信念来实现更好的多智能体协作。

Method: 提出了一种名为“可微信念对手塑形”（D-BOS）的一阶方法。该方法将观察者的信念视为待塑形的对手状态，通过 $k$ 步 Softmax-Bayes 信念动态进行微分，从而在信念更新路径上提供梯度信号，并能够通过聚合多个观察者的信念轨迹梯度来处理多智能体场景。

Result: 在隐藏角色游戏测试中，D-BOS 在性能上显著优于 PPO 和 BBM 等基准算法，特别是在涉及混合动机（mixed-motive）的复杂环境中表现出了最大的性能增益。

Conclusion: D-BOS 证明了将信念更新纳入梯度优化过程能够有效实现对手塑形。通过在信念空间中直接进行微分，该方法在复杂的多智能体隐藏角色游戏中展现了优于传统强化学习算法的适应性和协作表现，为解决多智能体协作与操纵问题提供了一种通用的数学框架。

Abstract: Human coordination often relies on the ability to influence the beliefs of others through strategic action. In multi-agent reinforcement learning, opponent shaping attempts to replicate this influence, though existing methods typically operate within an opponent's parameter, policy, or value space. Meanwhile, belief-manipulation techniques in hidden-role games often rely on hard-coded objectives, such as deception or belief saturation. We propose Differentiable Belief-based Opponent Shaping (D-BOS), a first-order method that treats each observer's belief as the shaped opponent state and differentiates through $k$-step softmax-Bayes belief dynamics. Rather than explicitly rewarding deceptive or cooperative behavior, our method treats the belief state as the target for shaping. This allows the optimal strategy to emerge naturally from the environment's reward structure. This belief-space formulation provides an opponent-shaping signal by differentiating through opponent belief updates, and naturally extends to multiple observers by aggregating gradients over their individual inferred belief trajectories. Empirically, D-BOS outperforms PPO and BBM in hidden-role games, with the largest gains in mixed-motive settings.

We propose an interpretable decision layer: a transparent mechanism that ranks course topics requiring attention without using grades or post-hoc outcome labels. The approach combines three signals: student learning difficulty prevalence, disagreement between learner self-reports and observed difficulties, and unresolved teacher concerns. The output is a ranked set of topic priorities with per-topic decision records explaining each ranking. In one graduate CS course offering ($n=5$ instructor interviews; $n=279$ survey responses), prioritized topics aligned with instructor concerns (top-5 overlap 3/5; Spearman $ρ=0.80$) and student-reported topic difficulty ($ρ=0.46$, $p=.048$). Multi-signal integration also surfaced learners not identified through individual signal sources alone (AUC $=0.96$ vs. $0.91$ for gap prevalence alone). Reflective thinking, help-seeking, and self-efficacy provided additional evidence that student behavioral signals align with learning-related constructs. While preliminary, these findings suggest that transparent coordination mechanisms may help support human-AI co-agency when feedback is incomplete.

*Diego Gosmar,Deborah A. Dahl*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一种集成连续记忆系统（CMS）与语义相似性缓存的嵌套学习架构，并采用“开放楼层协议”（OFP）协调的三阶段智能体流水线。通过五项关键性能指标（KPI）聚合为总幻觉分数（THS）来评估缓解与可观测性之间的权衡，并设计了非对称的审查机制（高随机性生成端+逐级校正端）进行验证。

Conclusion: 本文证明了基于记忆增强的多智能体架构（HOPE式嵌套学习与连续记忆系统）能够在无需模型重新训练的情况下，显著提升大型语言模型在多阶段流水线中的事实可靠性、运行效率及可审计性。研究结果表明，强化可观测性不仅不会削弱，反而能进一步增强幻觉缓解效果。

Abstract: Hallucination remains a major reliability barrier for production LLM systems, particularly in multi-agent pipelines where unsupported claims can propagate unchecked across stages. This paper adapts a HOPE-inspired Nested Learning architecture with Continuum Memory Systems (CMS) and semantic similarity caching to a hybrid benchmark of 310 prompts combining 217 epistemic-uncertainty prompts and 93 fabrication-induction stress-test prompts. A three-stage agentic pipeline orchestrated via the Open Floor Protocol (OFP) is evaluated with five KPIs -- FCD (Factual Claim Density), FGR (Factual Grounding References), FDF (Fictional Disclaimer Frequency), ECS (Explicit Contextualization Score), and OSR (Observability Score Ratio) -- aggregated into THS (Total Hallucination Score) across five weighting configurations to study mitigation-observability trade-offs. FDF, ECS, OSR, and FGR are subtracted as mitigation signals, so that a more negative THS indicates stronger mitigation. The FrontEndAgent is configured as a high-stochasticity generator (temperature = 1.0) to produce a realistic hallucination baseline, while the SecondLevelReviewer and ThirdLevelReviewer operate as progressive correctors. This asymmetric design yields end-to-end THS reductions of -31.3% to -35.9% across five weighting configurations. Semantic caching achieves 440 cache hits over 930 potential calls (47.3% hit rate), reducing LLM invocations to 490, lowering energy and CO2e footprint, and making multi-stage review pipelines operationally viable at production scale. ExtremeObservability attains the most negative final THS (-0.0709), confirming that observability-heavy configurations reinforce rather than compromise mitigation. These findings suggest that memory-augmented multi-agent designs can jointly improve factual reliability, operational efficiency, and auditability without model retraining.

### [142] [Robust and Efficient Guardrails with Latent Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29068)
*Siddharth Sai,Xiaofei Wen,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 COLAGUARD，这是一种新型大模型安全防御框架。它将多步安全推理压缩到潜在空间中，在保持高安全性能的同时，显著降低了推理延迟和计算成本，有效解决了现有推理驱动型防御机制难以在高吞吐场景中应用的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于推理的安全防护机制虽然性能优于单纯的分类模型，但因其需要显式生成推理过程（CoT），导致高昂的查询延迟和Token开销，难以满足高吞吐量的实际部署需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为 COLAGUARD 的防御框架。该方法通过阶段性的训练课程，将多步安全推理过程转化为连续的潜在空间表示，从而在推理时实现直接的隐藏状态传播，避免了显式生成推理文本所需的额外计算开销。

Conclusion: 潜在空间推理（Latent Reasoning）为构建高效、可部署的LLM安全防御机制提供了一种可行且有效的替代方案，证明了安全鲁棒性与推理效率可以实现同步优化，无需在两者之间进行权衡。

Abstract: Maintaining the safety of large language models (LLMs) is crucial as they are increasingly deployed in real-world applications. Existing safety guardrails typically rely on single-pass classification or, more recently, distilled reasoning. Reasoning-based guardrails significantly outperform classification-only baselines, but they incur substantial query latency and token overhead that make them impractical for highthroughput deployment. To address this challenge, we propose COLAGUARD, a guardrail model that transfers multi-step safety reasoning into a continuous latent space through a stage-wise training curriculum, enabling direct hidden-state propagation at inference. Evaluated on ten prompt- and response-moderation settings spanning eight safety benchmarks, COLAGUARD improves macro-F1 by 8.24 points over Llama Guard 3 and matches our explicit reasoning baseline, GuardReasoner, in macroF1 while delivering a 12.9X speedup and 22.4X reduction in token usage. Our results suggest that latent reasoning offers a practical alternative to explicit rationale generation for deployable guardrails, jointly improving safety robustness and inference efficiency rather than treating them as competing objectives.

### [143] [Bridging the Sim-to-Real Gap in Reinforcement Learning-Based Industrial Dispatching through Execution Semantics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29078)
*Jonathan Hoss,Noah Klarmann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种工业环境下策略中立的执行与测量中间层，通过标准化执行契约和差异化记录，解决了异步环境下调度决策的不可靠和不可解释性问题，有效提升了执行错误的可归因性与预防能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在工业环境中，事件驱动的调度策略常面临状态异步和部分观测的问题，导致决策状态在时间上不一致、操作准入性定义模糊以及执行错误难以追溯，从而限制了系统的可靠性和可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种策略中立的执行与测量层（Execution and Measurement Layer）。该层通过从异步事件流中构建决策有效的快照，定义具有明确操作准入性的标准化执行契约，并详细记录策略意图、事务结果、物理执行与人工干预之间的差异来实现目标。

Result: 离散事件仿真实验表明，该框架能将原本难以区分的执行失败转化为结构化、分类型的归因结果；在观测延迟较低的情况下，该框架能显著减少执行错误，实现错误的预防。

Conclusion: 本文提出的中间层架构成功地将复杂的工业环境下的执行不确定性转化为结构化的监控数据，为评估和优化调度策略提供了可靠的依据，有效提升了系统的可靠性与可解释性。

Abstract: Event-driven scheduling policies are increasingly deployed in industrial environments, where decisions are made under asynchronous and partially observed system states. As a result, decision states are not temporally consistent, action admissibility is not explicitly defined, and the origin of execution errors remains ambiguous. These issues limit both reliability and interpretability.
  To address this gap, a policy-neutral execution and measurement layer is proposed to mediate between scheduling policies and the industrial execution environment. The layer constructs decision-valid snapshots from asynchronous event streams, defines a standardized execution contract with explicit action admissibility, and records outcomes as divergences between policy intent, transactional outcomes, physical execution, and human intervention. This enables a separation between decision semantics and execution behavior and makes deployment mismatch observable and structurally attributable.
  The proposed framework is evaluated using a discrete-event simulation. The results show analytical benefits across all observation lag regimes, as undifferentiated execution failures are transformed into structured, typed outcomes with full attribution coverage. Operational benefits are strongest under low observation lag, where avoidable execution errors can be prevented before commitment. Overall, the layer turns execution uncertainty into supervisory data for evaluation and policy refinement.

</details>

In a random sample of 100 records, human and AI classifiers showed good agreement in identifying studies not substantively using AI, but lower agreement in classifying human-AI interaction, particularly where health professional interaction was ambiguous or insufficiently described. Overall, the results suggest that hybrid human-AI screening of clinical trial records is potentially viable, but clearer trial reporting and more precise interaction definitions will benefit the process.

### [145] [Xetrieval: Mechanistically Explaining Dense Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29507)
*Zhixin Cai,Jun Bai,Yang Liu,Jiaqi Li,Yichi Zhang,Taichuan Li,Zhuofan Chen,Zixia Jia,Zilong Zheng,Wenge Rong*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对稠密检索器“黑盒”问题，Xetrieval 通过在嵌入空间模拟思维链并分解出可解释的稀疏特征，实现了对检索决策的深层机制性解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稠密检索解释方法多依赖于表层特征（如词汇匹配），难以揭示深层高维嵌入背后的潜在逻辑，导致检索决策过程对用户而言是不透明的。

Method: 提出了 Xetrieval 框架：首先利用轻量级推理内化器在嵌入空间直接模拟思维链（Chain-of-Thought）推理，为句子嵌入注入推理信息；随后通过特征分解技术，将增强后的嵌入映射为稀疏且具有自然语言描述的解释性特征；最后通过跨视图的特征重叠聚合，实现对检索决策的细粒度解释。

Result: 实验证明，Xetrieval 不仅能提取出连贯且具备可解释性的特征，还在对检索对进行干预时表现出更强的因果效应，并支持通过特征调整来控制检索任务。

Conclusion: Xetrieval 提供了一种有效且高效的机制，能够深入解释稠密检索器在高维嵌入层面的决策机制，为理解复杂模型行为和实现可控检索提供了新工具。

Abstract: Explaining why dense retrievers assign high relevance scores remains challenging because retrieval decisions are made through opaque high-dimensional embeddings. Existing explanations often focus on surface signals, such as lexical matches, token alignments, or post-hoc textual rationales, and thus provide limited insight into the latent factors that shape dense retrieval behavior at the embedding level. We propose \textit{Xetrieval}, an embedding-level mechanistic framework for explaining dense retrieval. \textit{Xetrieval} first introduces a lightweight reasoning internalizer that approximates Chain-of-Thought reasoning directly in the embedding space with a single forward pass, enriching sentence embeddings with reasoning-oriented information while avoiding expensive autoregressive generation. It then decomposes these reasoning-enhanced embeddings into sparse, human-interpretable features, each associated with a coherent natural language description. By aggregating sparse feature overlaps across multiple document-side views, \textit{Xetrieval} provides feature-level explanations of individual retrieval decisions. Experiments on diverse retrievers and benchmarks show that \textit{Xetrieval} uncovers coherent interpretable features, yields stronger pair-level intervention effects, and supports task-level feature steering. The project page and source code are available at https://hihiczx.github.io/Xetrieval .

</details>


### [146] [PRO-CUA: Process-Reward Optimization for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29119)
*Yifei He,Rui Yang,Hao Bai,Tong Zhang,Han Zhao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算机使用智能体（CUA）的训练受限于昂贵的实时环境交互和高质量监督数据的匮乏，行为克隆存在分布偏移问题，而传统的轨迹级强化学习又面临奖励稀疏、信用分配模糊及高基础设施成本等挑战。

Method: 提出了 PRO-CUA 框架，核心在于通过过程奖励模型（PRM）提供分步反馈，解耦了在线环境交互与策略优化；利用当前策略生成候选动作并结合组内相对优势（group-relative advantages）进行优化，在无需离线专家轨迹的情况下实现密集且灵活的信用分配。

Result: 在实时 Web 基准测试中，PRO-CUA 证明了其有效性，显著优于传统方法，验证了基于 PRM 指导的分步训练能够提高智能体在复杂交互任务中的表现与可靠性。

Conclusion: PRO-CUA 通过引入过程奖励模型（PRM）和分步强化学习，有效解决了计算机使用智能体（CUA）在复杂工作流自动化中面临的训练效率低、分布偏移及奖励稀疏问题，为训练高性能、更可靠的智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: Computer use agents (CUAs) have shown strong potential for automating complex digital workflows, yet their training remains constrained by costly live environment interaction and limited high-quality supervision. Existing filtered behavior cloning pipelines suffer from imitation bottlenecks, including distribution shift from the expert demonstration and the absence of negative learning signals. Meanwhile, standard trajectory-level reinforcement learning struggles with sparse rewards, ambiguous credit assignment, and high infrastructure costs for long-horizon GUI interaction. In this work, we propose PRO-CUA, a process-reward optimization framework for training CUAs with iterative step-level reinforcement learning. PRO-CUA decouples on-policy environment interaction from policy optimization: the current policy collects states through live rollouts, generates diverse candidate actions for each state, receives step-level feedback from a process reward model (PRM), and is optimized with group-relative advantages. This design enables dense and flexible credit assignment without relying on golden answers or offline expert trajectories, while reducing distribution shift by training on the agent's own execution states. Experiments on live web benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of PRO-CUA and the reliability of PRM-guided step-level training.

### [147] [HiKEY: Hierarchical Multimodal Retrieval for Open-Domain Document Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29606)
*Joongmin Shin,Gyuho Shim,Jeongbae Park,Jaehyung Seo,Heuiseok Lim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对工业文档检索中定位难和碎片化的问题，HiKEY 提出了一种利用文档层级结构进行多模态检索的框架，通过结构化解析和粗到细的检索策略，显著提升了检索召回率和问答准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于文档切片或页面图像的检索方法在处理大规模工业语料时存在“路由失效”（难以定位目标文档）和“证据碎片化”（难以整合跨度大的表格、图表信息）两大瓶颈，导致检索精度和问答效果受限。

Method: 提出了一种基于层级树的检索框架 HiKEY：1. 使用文档层级解析（DHP）重构异构图，明确父子关系；2. 实施粗到细的检索策略，先进行层级化全局路由剪枝，再通过多模态融合进行细粒度检索；3. 采用混合结构-语义打包策略，构建高信息密度的证据子图。

Result: 在开放域问答（ODQA）基准测试中，HiKEY 显著优于基于页面或切片的基准方法，检索召回率提升最高达 12.9%，端到端问答性能提升最高达 6.8%。

Conclusion: HiKEY 通过引入层级化结构感知和异构图表示，有效地解决了工业级文档检索中的定位难和信息碎片化问题，为复杂多模态文档的知识检索提供了高效且准确的新范式。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) for document-based Open-domain Question Answering (ODQA) on large-scale industrial corpora faces two critical bottlenecks: routing failure in locating the correct document and evidence fragmentation in integrating scattered information. Existing approaches relying on flat text chunks or page-level images inherently struggle to (i) precisely pinpoint the target document among thousands of candidates and (ii) organically connect multimodal evidence, such as tables and figures, within a limited token budget. To address these challenges, we propose HiKEY, a hierarchical tree-based multimodal retrieval framework that elevates document hierarchy to a first-class retrieval signal. Instead of simple chunking, HiKEY reconstructs a logical heterogeneous graph via Document Hierarchical Parsing (DHP), explicitly encoding parent-child relationships. Adopting a hierarchical coarse-to-fine strategy, the framework (1) performs global routing to rapidly prune the search space using hierarchical indexing, and (2) conducts fine-grained retrieval to rank sections by employing a multimodal fusion strategy that captures the most discriminative evidence. Finally, HiKEY assembles a token-efficient evidence subgraph via a hybrid structural-semantic packing strategy. Experiments on ODQA benchmarks demonstrate that HiKEY significantly outperforms page- and chunk-based baselines, improving retrieval recall by up to 12.9% and end-to-end QA performance by up to 6.8%.

### [148] [The Confidence Shortcut: A Reasoning Failure Mode of Masked Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29123)
*Dueun Kim,Albert No*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了掩码扩散语言模型（MDM）中“置信度对齐”训练策略的副作用：在复杂的逻辑推理任务中，该策略会破坏任务所需的逻辑流，导致模型在困难样本上产生高置信度错误；而传统的随机掩码训练反而能更好地保留推理轨迹，提升模型的稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前MDM普遍采用基于置信度的解码策略，且近期的训练方案倾向于使训练掩码模式与解码模式对齐。研究者发现这种做法在逻辑推理任务中是反效果的，因为置信度解码倾向于优先预测局部容易的Token，从而破坏了复杂推理所需的逻辑流和长程依赖。

Method: 研究者通过对比实验，分析了掩码扩散语言模型（MDM）在不同训练策略（置信度对齐训练 vs. 随机掩码训练）下，针对多位数加法等需要逻辑推理的任务的表现。重点探讨了基于置信度的解码策略如何导致模型在处理复杂输入时出现局部预测错误，并量化了不同训练方式对错误率的影响。

Result: 研究发现，置信度对齐训练会将模型在复杂推理任务上的错误率扩大一个数量级。在五个不同的推理任务中，置信度解码均会导致模型在复杂输入上产生“高置信度错误”，而随机掩码策略则能有效地保持推理逻辑的连贯性，在处理困难样本时表现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 基于置信度的解码策略在处理复杂逻辑推理任务时存在内在缺陷，而与之对齐的训练策略反而会加剧模型在困难任务上的错误率。相比之下，传统的随机掩码策略虽然效率较低，但能更好地保留推理轨迹的依赖关系，对于解决长程依赖问题更为稳健。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models (MDMs) uniquely support any-order generation, with confidence-based decoding currently serving as the de facto standard inference policy. To optimize for this, recent training schemes attempt to align training mask patterns directly with those observed during generation. However, we argue that confidence-based decoding is inherently misaligned with the logical-flow trajectories required for complex reasoning, and that confidence-aligned training actively entrenches this misalignment. We make this concrete using multi-digit addition, where the decoding strategy prematurely predicts locally easy digits before resolving their long-range dependencies, producing high-confidence errors on challenging inputs. While traditional random masking keeps the failure rate low on this challenging tail, confidence-aligned training amplifies the error rate by an order of magnitude. Across five distinct reasoning tasks, this same pattern emerges with task-dependent severity: confidence-based decoding induces failures on highly complex inputs, and confidence-aligned training exacerbates them. In contrast, random masking -- despite its perceived inefficiency -- robustly preserves the reasoning-trajectory conditionals essential for solving the challenging tail.

### [149] [Better Later Than Sooner: Neuro-Symbolic Knowledge Graph Construction via Ontology-grounded Post-extraction Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29168)
*Lorenzo Loconte,Timothy Hospedales,Cristina Cornelio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有RAG方法在复杂推理和符号运算上的不足，本文提出了一种本体导向的神经符号框架，通过规范化和后期纠错机制，在降低计算开销的同时构建出更高质量、更符合本体逻辑的知识图谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的检索增强生成（RAG）方法难以可靠地处理需要多跳推理或符号运算（如聚合、列表）的复杂查询。基于符号的知识图谱方法虽然支持SQL类查询，但现有的利用LLM提取知识图谱的流程往往会导致事实与常识本体约束冲突，且存在计算效率低的问题。

Method: 提出了一种神经符号化框架，包括三个核心步骤：(1) 从开放领域进行知识提取；(2) 利用嵌入技术对实体类型和谓词进行规范化（canonicalization）；(3) 针对本体违规（ontology violations）进行有针对性的LLM修正。这种方法通过将纠错步骤推迟到提取后期，减少了重复调用LLM的需求。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够有效减少LLM的Token使用量，大幅提升知识图谱的一致性，同时保持了下游问答任务的质量，并被证明非常适合通过SPARQL图模式进行符号化查询。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的本体导向神经符号框架能够有效解决从非结构化文本中提取知识图谱时存在的逻辑一致性问题，同时通过优化的后处理修正流程，在降低计算成本的同时显著提升了知识图谱的质量，为复杂推理和符号化查询提供了可靠的基础。

Abstract: Question answering (QA) is a core challenge in AI, particularly for complex queries requiring multi-hop reasoning across documents, or symbolic operations like aggregation or exhaustive listing. Retrieval-augmented generation has become the dominant approach to QA, with recent graph-based variants addressing part of these issues by organizing knowledge to better support compositional questions. However, most textual graph-based RAG methods still lack the structure needed for symbolic operations useful to answer complex questions reliably. This motivates symbolic graph-based approaches, which extract knowledge graphs (KGs) whose relations are logic predicates that enable SQL-like querying. Yet these pipelines typically use LLMs for KG extraction, which can introduce consistency issues, where extracted facts may violate commonsense ontology constraints. We propose a neuro-symbolic framework for ontology-grounded KG construction combining open-domain extraction, embedding-based canonicalization of types and predicates, and targeted LLM-based correction of ontology violations. By deferring corrections to a post-extraction stage, our method avoids repeated LLM calls, substantially reducing token usage while improving KG consistency and preserving downstream QA quality. Finally, we show that the extracted KGs are well suited for symbolic querying by measuring the occurrence of SPARQL graph patterns.

### [150] [BenchTrace: A Benchmark for Testing Reflection Ability and Controlled Evolution in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29225)
*Jiahao Huang,Fei Cheng,Junfeng Jiang,Zefan Yu,Akiko Aizawa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BenchTrace是一个专门评估LLM智能体自我进化能力的新型基准，通过故障识别QA和故障规避仿真，揭示了智能体在诊断、记忆保持和泛化方面的具体缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了包含1821个标注片段的快照反射数据集；设计了“反射评估”（通过目标QA测试故障识别能力）和“进化评估”（在受控环境下测试故障规避行为）；提出了“故障规避率”（FAR）作为新的核心评估指标，并进行了相关性分析。

Result: Qwen3-32B和GPT-4.1在反射评估中的端到端通过率不足30%，诊断能力是主要瓶颈；实验表明自我进化虽能提高FAR，但存在“遗忘”和“负迁移”现象；研究还发现，只有完全正确的反射与更高的FAR显著相关。

Abstract: Self-evolving agents improve over time by reflecting on past failures, but existing evaluation is limited in two ways: it measures only task scores, leaving reflection quality unknown, and it relies on agents' own episode runs, offering no mechanism to target specific failure patterns. We present \textbf{BenchTrace}, a benchmark for evaluating self-evolution ability in LLM agents. BenchTrace is built on a snapshot-reflection dataset of 1,821 annotated episodes spanning six diverse tasks, and comprises a \textbf{Reflection Evaluation} that probes failure identification through targeted QA tasks, and an \textbf{Evolution Evaluation} that tests whether past failure experience translates into avoidance behavior in a controlled self-evolution simulation. Building on BenchTrace, we propose \textbf{failure avoidance rate (FAR)}, a new evaluation metric measuring the fraction of test cases in which the agent successfully avoids the target failure instance. Experiments with Qwen3-32B and GPT-4.1 reveal that both models fall below a 30\% end-to-end pass rate on reflection evaluation, with diagnosis as the primary bottleneck. Evolution evaluation shows that self-evolution methods generally improve FAR over the non-evolving baseline, but agents forget early lessons as noise episodes accumulate, and agents fail to generalize their reflections beyond the specific context, causing negative transfer across task contexts. Our correlation analysis further reveals that only a fully correct reflection is strongly associated with higher FAR. BenchTrace exposes concrete limits of current self-evolution approaches and provides a controlled, model-agnostic framework for targeted evaluation.

### [151] [Tailoring the Curriculum: Student-Centered Reasoning Distillation via Dynamic Data-Model Compatibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.29229)
*Jiahao Huang,Fei Cheng,Junfeng Jiang,Akiko Aizawa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文引入了数据-模型兼容性（DMC）指标，通过量化数据与学生模型间的匹配度，实现了推理蒸馏中数据的高效筛选与动态优化，显著提升了蒸馏性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理蒸馏的成功高度依赖于训练数据与学生模型之间的匹配程度，但目前缺乏有效的定量评估方法来衡量这种兼容性，导致蒸馏过程往往盲目且低效。

Method: 提出了一种名为数据-模型兼容性（DMC）的评估指标，该指标综合考虑了数据质量、任务相对难度以及学生模型自身的推理能力。研究通过评估DMC与蒸馏性能的相关性，以及基于DMC进行动态数据选择来验证该方法的有效性。
